* Die Nutzung der folgenden Luraumdaten
* entbindet nicht von der gesetzlichen
* Verpflichtung der gewissenhaen und

* Verwendung aller notwendigen und zugelassenen
* Navigationsmittel (z. B. Lufahrtkarte ICAO 1:500.000).
*
* Bundeskommission Segelflug im
* Deutschen Aero Club e.V.
*
*
*
* LEGAL DISCLAIMER
* The use of the following airspace data
* does not release the pilot from his legal
* obligation of thorough and orderly preflight
* planning, nor from the use of all required
* and approved means of navigation
* (e.g. Aeronautical Chart ICAO 1:500.000).
*
* Bundeskommission Segelflug im
* Deutschen Aero Club e.V.
*
* effective from 31st March 2016
* All data and information contained in this data file is provided without guarantee as to their completeness or correctness.   
* Any conclusions drawn from these data and information are the sole responsibility of the user.
* 
* ATTENTION:  Airspace referring to aerodromes outside germany is NOT included in this file !!!
*             e.g. Airspace C LFSB, etc.
*
*
* The times for the restricted and danger areas (ED-R´s and ED-D´s) are from German-AIP.
* 
*   e.g.    MON-THU     = this area is active from Monday till Thursday 
*           MON-FRI+    = this area is normally active from Monday till Friday. Activation for SAT, SUN and HOL is possible by NOTAM
*                         Special times [e.g. MON 0600 (0500)-FRI 1300(1200)] are NOT indicated!!
*           NOTAM       = this area will only be activated by NOTAM
*           H24         = this area is 24hours every day active including holidays!!
*           HX          = undefined activation times, activation is possible on short notice at every time
*
* Changes to this times can be distributed at every time by NOTAM
*
*
*########################################################################################################
*########################################################################################################
*
*
*
* changes CW50/14 -> CW14/15 (AIRAC)
* CTR EDAC downgraded to RMZ, RMZ EDBN new
* CTR EDDK changed coordinates
* D (not CTR) EDFH changed and EDDK new
* TMZ EDFH new
* ED-R76 new coordinates, new sectors, new glidersector "Boxberg"
* ED-R60 new
* C EDDK + EDDF modified
* glider sectors "Loccum" withdrawn
* glider sector "Landshut" new dimension
*
* changes CW14/15 -> CW18/15
* EDDB-CTR changed coordinates during usage of southern RWY
*
* changes CW18/15 -> CW23/15
* ED-R 110 + 115 withdrawn
*
* changes CW23/15 -> CW47/15
* EDDB-CTR back to old dimension, southern RWY clsd 
* EDRZ CTR replaced by RMZ
* ED-R Reit im Winkl added (activation by NOTAM possible between 01Dec15 until 31Mar16)
*
* changes CW47/15 -> CW13/16
* EDFE: CTR withdrawn, now combined TMZ/RMZ/ATZ with new coordinates
* ED-R33, 138, 144 and 147 modified coordinates/upper limits 
* RMZ EDWB withdrawn
* TMZ EDDN new coordinates, glider sector Seckendorf-Ansbach new dimensions
* TMZ EDDR new coordinates
* CTR EDDF+EDDM new coordinates
* D (not CTR) EDDH withdrawn, C extended
* D (not CTR)/C EDDV new dimension
* D (not CTR) EDDS new dimension
*
* changes CW13/16 -> CW22/16
* LSZH added, but only airspace overhead germany and close to swiss/german border
*
